the authorized amount to be incurred by recognized political parties, independent groups, and other candidates contesting 
the Local authorities election - 2023 to elect members to every Municipal Council, Urban council, and Pradeshiya sabha 
established under a written law in pursuance of the provisions of the Local authorities elections Ordinance (Chapter 262), 
for Election propaganda activities within each electoral area, as fixed by the Election Commission in Consultation with

03 of the Regulation of Election Expenditure Act, No. 03 of 2023, is indicated in the Schedule below.

Part I : Sec. (I) - GaZette eXtRaORdINaRy OF the deMOCRatIC sOCIaLIst RePUBLIC OF sRI LaNKa - 25.01.2023
2a
the  sChedULe  aBOve  ReFeRRed  tO
 01.  a candidate contesting the said election may incur not more than Rs. 20/- per elector registered in the valid 
electoral register of his ward as his campaign expenses in the ward in which he is contesting. Accordingly, the 
maximum limit of expenditure to be incurred by a candidate contesting each ward is shown below. (The relevant 
authorized amount is given in Annexure-01).
 02. a  recognized political party or an independent group may incur a sum of 60% of the amount resulting from the 
multiplication of the total number of registered voters in the electoral area of the local authority for the current 
year by Rs. 20/-, the sum fixed to be incurred by each candidate contesting the Election per elector registered 
in the valid electoral register, as campaign expenses for contesting that local authority. (The relevant authorized 
amount is given in Annexure - 02)
 03. t he sum of 40% of the amount resulting from the multiplication of the total number of registered voters in the 
electoral area by Rs. 20/-, the sum fixed to be incurred per elector registered in the valid electoral register for 
the electoral area of the local authority, divided by the total number of candidates in the 
second nomination 
list, shall be the authorized amount to be incurred by an additional candidate. (the relevant authorized amount 
is given in Annexure - 03).
 04. t he relevant recognized political party, independent group, or candidate shall submit the audited returns of 
expenditure within twenty-one days of the date of publication of the result of the Election to the returning 
officer of the respective local authority. The return shall be signed by the candidate and attested by a Justice of 
the Peace.
  t he return should state the amount of every donation or contribution accepted or received by or on behalf of 
the recognized political party, independent group, or candidate, and if the donation or contribution is in kind, 
the estimated value of the donation or contribution; 
whether such donation or contribution was by way of gift, 
loan, advance or deposit; and the name, address and National Identity Card number or registration number as 
the case may be, of the individual or body of persons incorporated or unincorporated making such donation or 
contribution.
  The return shall include expenditure incurred by or on behalf of the candidate, whether paid or unpaid for-
 (a) The Printing, publication, pasting, exhibition, or display of, advertisements, handbills, flags, drawings, 
photographs, placards, or posters;
 (b) t he production and broadcast, on radio or television of advertisements;
 (c) t he production and publication in newspapers, journals, or other publications of advertisements;
 (d) t he hiring or use of any premises or equipment for the holding of meetings; and
 (e) t he provision of fuel for the running of vehicles;
  Together with bills and receipts confirming the same, and if the above services were obtained without payment, 
the names and the addresses of the persons from whom such services were obtained shall be included.
  However, the expenditure incurred by or on behalf of the candidate for
 (a) t he transport of the candidate within the area for which the election is being held; and 
 (b) t he stationery, telephone, or other means of communication,
 shall not be included in the return.

<!-- page 3 -->

I fldgi ( ^I& fPoh - YS% ,xld m%cd;dka;s%l iudcjd§ ckrcfha w;s úfYI .eiÜ m;%h - 2023'01'25
Part I : Sec. (I) - GaZette eXtRaORdINaRy OF the deMOCRatIC sOCIaLIst RePUBLIC OF sRI LaNKa - 25.01.2023
3a
 05. On receipt of the returns, the respective returning Officer or the Election Commission shall cause a notice to be 
published  within ten (10) days in at least one newspaper in the sinhala, tamil, and english languages stating 
that the returning officer or the Election Commission has received the returns and declarations and indicating 
the place and time at which such returns and declarations may be inspected by any person.
 06. a ny person can obtain copies of such returns or declarations on payment of a fee from the respective returning 
officers.
 07. Every political party, independent group, or candidate that fails to submit returns on the specified date or makes 
erroneous returns commits and offence of an illegal practice and shall be liable to penalties specified by the Local 
authorities elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) as amended by the act, No. 16 of 2017, for the commission of 
an illegal practice. 
 08. (1) a  recognized political party, independent group, or candidate at this Local authorities election, shall not 
accept or receive a donation or contribution whether such donation or contribution is in cash or kind from-
 (a) a  Government department, a public Corporation, or a company incorporated under the Companies 
act, No. 7 of 2007, or under any former written law relating to companies in which the government or 
a public Corporation owns any shares;
 (b) a  foreign government, an international organization, or a body corporate incorporated or registered 
outside sri Lanka;
 (c) a  Company incorporated in sri Lanka under the Companies act, No. 7 of 2007 or under any former 
written law relating to Companies where the foreign shareholding in such Company, either direct or 
indirect, is fifty percent or above ; or
 (d) a ny person whose identity is not disclosed, for the purpose of promoting or procuring the election of 
such recognized political party, independent group or candidate at such election.
  (2) A candidate who contravenes the provisions of Subsection (1) commits an offence of an illegal practice 
within the meaning of the Local authorities elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) as amended by the act, No. 
16 of 2017, and shall be liable to the penalties imposed under the Ordinance in respect of the offence of an 
illegal practice.
